createInstance = {import:create-instance-plugin}

title
  Lazy GM's Random Generator

generator_type = monument
setting = None 
spelltype = no_spell

output
  {A} [monument_output] ^[generator_type == "monument"]
  {A} [ancestral_monument_output] ^[generator_type == "ancestral_monument"]
  {A} [monument_of_power_output] ^[generator_type == "monument_of_power"]
  {A} [location_output] ^[generator_type == "location"]
  {A} [item_output] ^[generator_type == "item"]
  [npc_output] ^[generator_type == "npc"]
  [encounter_output] ^[generator_type == "encounter"]
  [quest_output] ^[generator_type == "quest"]
  [Roll1 = D100.selectOne.evaluateItem,Roll2 = D100.selectOne.evaluateItem,""] [Coins=createInstance(CoinsT1), Coins.Description] (["<b>"][Math.floor(Coins.Value)]gp["</b>"]); [Roll=Roll1,TreasureT1][Legend==1 ? ", " : ""][Roll=Roll2, Legend==1 ? TreasureT1 : ""] ["<b>"][TreasureValue]gp["</b>"]; [Roll=Roll1,MagicItemsT1][Legend==1 ? ", " : ""][Roll=Roll2, Legend==1 ? MagicItemsT1 : ""][TreasureValue=0,""] ^[generator_type == "tier_1_treasure_hoard"]
  [Roll1 = D100.selectOne.evaluateItem,Roll2 = D100.selectOne.evaluateItem,""] [Coins=createInstance(CoinsT2), Coins.Description] (["<b>"][Math.floor(Coins.Value)]gp["</b>"]); [Roll=Roll1,TreasureT2][Legend==1 ? ", " : ""][Roll=Roll2, Legend==1 ? TreasureT2 : ""] ["<b>"][TreasureValue]gp["</b>"]; [Roll=Roll1,MagicItemsT2][Legend==1 ? ", " : ""][Roll=Roll2, Legend==1 ? MagicItemsT2 : ""][TreasureValue=0,""] ^[generator_type == "tier_2_treasure_hoard"]
  [Roll1 = D100.selectOne.evaluateItem,Roll2 = D100.selectOne.evaluateItem,""] [Coins=createInstance(CoinsT3), Coins.Description] (["<b>"][Math.floor(Coins.Value)]gp["</b>"]); [Roll=Roll1,TreasureT3][Legend==1 ? ", " : ""][Roll=Roll2, Legend==1 ? TreasureT3 : ""] ["<b>"][TreasureValue]gp["</b>"]; [Roll=Roll1,MagicItemsT3][Legend==1 ? ", " : ""][Roll=Roll2, Legend==1 ? MagicItemsT3 : ""][TreasureValue=0,""] ^[generator_type == "tier_3_treasure_hoard"]
  [Roll1 = D100.selectOne.evaluateItem,Roll2 = D100.selectOne.evaluateItem,""] [Coins=createInstance(CoinsT4), Coins.Description] (["<b>"][Math.floor(Coins.Value)]gp["</b>"]); [Roll=Roll1,TreasureT4][Legend==1 ? ", " : ""][Roll=Roll2, Legend==1 ? TreasureT4 : ""] ["<b>"][TreasureValue]gp["</b>"]; [Roll=Roll1,MagicItemsT4][Legend==1 ? ", " : ""][Roll=Roll2, Legend==1 ? MagicItemsT4 : ""][TreasureValue=0,""] ^[generator_type == "tier_4_treasure_hoard"]
  [element.sentenceCase] [trap] and [element] [trap] triggered by [trigger]. ^[generator_type == "trap"]
  [unique_magic_weapon] ^ [generator_type == "unique_magic_weapon"]
  [unique_magic_armor] ^ [generator_type == "unique_magic_armor"]
  [lgm_cr_0_4_treasure] ^[generator_type == "lgm_cr_0_4_treasure"]
  [lgm_cr_5_10_treasure] ^[generator_type == "lgm_cr_5_10_treasure"]
  [lgm_cr_11_16_treasure] ^[generator_type == "lgm_cr_11_16_treasure"]
  [lgm_cr_17plus_treasure] ^[generator_type == "lgm_cr_17plus_treasure"]
  [lgm_tier_1] ^[generator_type == "lgm_tier_1"]
  [lgm_tier_2] ^[generator_type == "lgm_tier_2"]
  [lgm_tier_3] ^[generator_type == "lgm_tier_3"]
  [lgm_tier_4] ^[generator_type == "lgm_tier_4"]

unique_magic_weapon
  A [weapons] [spell]

unique_magic_armor
  A suit of [armor] [spell]

monument_output
  [condition.selectUnique(2).joinItems(" ")] [monument] [setting_select] [spell]
  
monument_of_power_output
  [condition.selectUnique(2).joinItems(" ")] [monument] [monument_effect]

item_output
  [condition] [origin] [item] [setting_select] [spell] ^[setting == "None"]
  
encounter_output
  [situation]

dmg_magic_item_output
  [wotc_srd_magic_items] 

npc_output
  [name] [surname_first][surname_last], {a} [personality] [race] [setting_select]

location_output
  [condition] [origin] [location] [setting_select]

situation
  [random_monsters.sentenceCase] are burying {a} [item_output] at {a} [monument_output]
  [random_monsters.sentenceCase] have been slain by [random_monsters] at {a} [monument_output]
  [random_monsters.sentenceCase] are about to arrive at {a} [monument_output]
  [random_monsters.sentenceCase] already passed by {a} [monument_output]
  [random_monsters.sentenceCase] are found dead at {a} [monument_output]
  [random_monsters.sentenceCase] are engaged in a ritual at {a} [monument_output]
  [random_monsters.sentenceCase] are digging for {a} [item_output] at {a} [monument_output]
  [random_monsters.sentenceCase] are camping at {a} [monument_output]
  [random_monsters.sentenceCase] are preparing an ambush at {a} [monument_output]
  [random_monsters.sentenceCase] are engaged in drunken revelry at {a} [monument_output]
  [random_monsters.sentenceCase] capturing [random_monsters] at {a} [monument_output]
  [random_monsters.sentenceCase] are in a battle with [random_monsters] at {a} [monument_output]
  [random_monsters.sentenceCase] are hunting for [random_monsters] at {a} [monument_output]
  [random_monsters.sentenceCase] are hunting for the characters at {a} [monument_output]
  [random_monsters.sentenceCase] are found dead along side [random_monsters] at {a} [monument_output]
  [random_monsters.sentenceCase] and [random_monsters] battle each other at {a} [monument_output]
  Friendly [random_monsters] are found at {a} [monument_output]
  [random_monsters.sentenceCase] are playing around at {a} [monument_output]
  [random_monsters.sentenceCase] are singing at {a} [monument_output]
  [random_monsters.sentenceCase] are building something at {a} [monument_output]
  [random_monsters.sentenceCase] wounded by [random_monsters] recover at {a} [monument_output]
  [random_monsters.sentenceCase] are running from [random_monsters] at {a} [monument_output]

setting_select
  ^[setting == "None"]
  of [cult_faction] ^[setting == "dnd_cult"]
  of [midgard_faction] ^[setting == "midgard"]
  of [eberron_faction] ^[setting == "eberron"]
  of [fr_faction] ^[setting == "fr"]
  of [generic_faction] ^[setting == "generic"]
  of [domain_of_dread] ^[setting == "domain_of_dread"]
  of [ebon_tides_faction] ^[setting == "ebontides"]
  of the [spelljammer_faction] ^[setting == "spelljammer"]
  of [southlands_gods] ^[setting == "southlands"]
  of [greyhawk_factions] ^[setting == "greyhawk"]
  of [city_of_arches_factions] ^[setting == "city_of_arches"]
  of [theros_factions] ^[setting == "theros"]
  of [exandria_gods] ^[setting == "exandria"]

spell
  ^[spelltype == "no_spell"]
  that casts [a5e_spells] ^[spelltype == "a5e_spells"]
  that casts [phb_5e_spells] ^[spelltype == "phb_5e_spells"]
  that casts [deep_magic_spell] ^[spelltype == "deep_magic_spell"]
  that casts [deep_magic_2023_spells] ^[spelltype == "deep_magic_2023_spell"]

quest_output
  [npc_output], wants the characters to [mission_objective]

mission_objective
  retrieve {a} [item_output], held by [adversaries] at {a} [location_set]
  hunt down {a} [npc_output], protected by [humanoids] at {a} [location_set]
  clear out [random_monsters] at {a} [location_set]
  rescue {a} [npc_output], imprisoned by [adversaries] at {a} [location_set]

location_set
  [condition] [condition] [location] [setting_select]

adversaries  
  {[humanoids]|[random_monsters]}

random_monsters
  [monster_conditions] {[cr_quarter]^2|[cr_half]^2|[cr_1]|[cr_2]|[cr_3]|[cr_4_5]^0.5}s
  
random_traps
  [condition] [trap] and [condition] [trap] triggered by a [trap_trigger].

city_of_arches_factions
  Arazuun, Fallen Prince of Revvia (Upper fanged jaw dripping acid. Chaotic evil demon prince of war pulled from the depths of the abyss after the fall of the Nameless King. Former lord of Revvia.)
  the Black Hand (Hand clutching a black dagger point downward. Neutral evil god of theft, trickery, and murder. Also the name of the largest thieves guild and artifact hunters in the City of Arches.)
  Elvenya the Star’s Song (Finger pointing towards a distant star. Neutral good elven god of knowledge and light worshipped by the Starlit Elves.)
  the Archkeepers (Basket of breads and cheeses. A lawful good order of knowledge serving those who step through the arches, providing food, shelter, and safety for confused travelers.)
  God-queen Sett (Hooded pair of burning eyes. Chaotic evil sorcerer queen of forbidden magic queen and consort of the Nameless King.)
  the Hunger (Black tentacles reaching out of black water. Neutral evil tempest-domain kraken lurking in Blackwater Caverns in the Revlend Marshes.)
  Ibraxus of Choul (Four-fingered hand holding a bleeding skull. Chaotic evil demon prince of war and death who gave the Nameless King much of the lich’s power.)
  Karigulon the Dread Fang (Profile of a roaring hyena head blood dripping from mouth. Chaotic evil demon of war and death worshipped by the gnolls of Blackmoon Hollow in the Doorish Hills.)
  Lady Straythe (White glove speckled with blood. Lawful evil vampire queen of the blood and death domain residing in Castle Nightfall in the Doorish Hills.)
  the Lower Twelve (Twelve black candles surrounding a half-pentagram. Twelve lawful, neutral, and chaotic evil deities of war, trickery, and death worshipped by the followers of the Nameless King.)
  Mother Avanta (Flame-wreathed curved fang. Neutral-aligned ancient red dragon of the domains of fire who once laired in Sunken Revvia.)
  the Nameless King (Charred crowned skull. Neutral evil ruler over the City of Arches and its surrounding lands over a thousand years ago.)
  Predalion, God of Travel and Trade (Wagon wheel behind crossed wheat chaffs. Lawful good deity of nature and knowledge worshipped in the Doorish Hills.)
  Sulin, Goddess of Light (Eight-pointed star. Lawful good deity of light and life worshipped in the Village of Peat in the Doorish Hills.)
  the Three Sisters (Silhouette of the statues of three sisters, heads bowed and hands outstretched. Three lawful, neutral, and chaotic good goddesses named Levyl, Kryssa, and Dura of the domains of life, knowledge, and death respectively.)
  Vithra the Serpent King (Hooded and fanged serpent head. Neutral evil god of serpents and reptiles worshipped in the Western Deadlands at the Idol of the Serpent King.)
  Vrys the Fallen (Weeping mouthless face. Lawful evil fallen deva of darkness and knowledge residing in the ruined tower of Gray Reach in Sunken Revvia.)
  the World’s End (Horned skull with humanoid skull in its jaws. Chaotic evil massive civilization- destroying beast whose skull lies half buried in the Revlend Marshes.)
  Xereth – Oblivion’s End (Profile of draconic skull wreathed in black flame. Chaotic evil ancient undead red dragon and former mount of the Nameless King.)
  Xrake Fiendblood (Draconic head floating over a pool of acid dripping from its mouth. Neutral evil ancient fiendish black dragon who warred with the archmage Tryvanus of Krate in Sunken Revvia.)  

midgard_faction
  Veles the Great Serpent (<em>Midgard Worldbook</em> 348)
  Freyr and Freyja the Twin Northern Gods of Passion, Fertility, Magic, and the Living World (<em>Midgard Worldbook</em> 350)
  Loki the Northern Trickster God of Cunning, Mischief and Malice (<em>Midgard Worldbook</em> 351)
  Sif the Northern Sword Maiden (<em>Midgard Worldbook</em> 352)

monument_effect
  of fury: All creatures have advantage on melee attacks.  
  of sundering: All creatures are -4 to AC.  
  of flames: All creatures add 1d4 fire damage to non-magical melee or ranged attacks per 5 CR.  
  of thunderbolts: All creatures add 1d4 lightning damage to non-magical melee or ranged attacks per 5 CR.  
  of frost: All creatures add 1d4 cold damage to non-magical melee or ranged attacks per 5 CR.  
  of poison: All creatures add 1d4 poison damage to non-magical melee or ranged attacks per 5 CR.  
  of antimagic: All creatures have disadvantage on magic attack rolls, and have advantage on saving throws vs. magic.  
  of arcane might: All creatures have advantage on spell attacks, and disadvantage on magical saving throws.  
  of speed: All creatures have double movement speed and can take one extra melee attack per turn.  
  of blessings: All creatures can add +1d4 to all d20 rolls.  
  of undeath: All creatures receive half healing from healing effects.  
  of enervation: All creatures have disadvantage on melee attacks.  
  of fog: All creatures have disadvantage on ranged attacks.  
  of weakness: All creatures have disadvantage on str, dex, or con saving throws.  
  of screams: All creatures have disadvantage on int, wis, or cha saving throws.  
  of ooze: All creatures move at half speed.  
  of searing beams: Any creature that ends its turn and hasn't moved 15 feet takes 5 damage per tier.  
  of arcane protection: Any spellcaster gains +2 to AC.  
  of bloodshed: Attacks score a critical hit on an 18, 19, or 20.  
  of empowerment: All magic weapons and armor gain an additional +1.  
  of vengeance: Creatures gain +2 to attack and damage against creatures within five feet of an ally.  
  of the beast: All creatures have +2 to melee attack rolls but are -2 to AC.  
  of the berserker: All melee attacks gain +5 damage.  
  of holy light: The melee and ranged attacks of all living creatures gain +1d4 radiant damage per 5 CR.  

southlands_gods
  Bes – Lord of Dwarves, Husband to Taweret, Protector of the Household, and Lord of Lions  (<em>Southlands</em> 225)
  Hune – Lord of Doors, Patron of Portals, and Ancient Keeper of the Labyrinth  (<em>Southlands</em> 225)
  Khonsu – Prince of the Moon, Master of Passage of Time, Guardian of Night Travelers, Lord of Dice, Binder of Wounds, and Falcon of the Gods  (<em>Southlands</em> 226)
  Shu – Invisible Lord of Wind and Sky, King of Clouds, Lord of Lions, Peaceful Ruler of the Sky, and Grandfather of Osiris, Set, and Isis  (<em>Southlands</em> 226)
  Sobek - God of Rivers and Crocodiles, Patron of the Subek, Lord of Lakes and Marshes (<em>Southlands</em> 227)
  Taweret - Goddess of Hippos, Wife of Bes, and Wife of Set (<em>Southlands</em> 227)
  Wadjet - Mother of Cobras, Seer to the Gods, and Guardian of the Subek (<em>Southlands</em> 228)
  Anu-Akma – God of the Underworld, Judge of the Dead and Guardian of Tombs, Guide of the People of Khem, Purifier of Souls, Preserver of the Worthy, King of Jackals, and Patron of the Gnolls and Ghouls (<em>Southlands</em> 232)
  Aten – Sun God, Jealous Lord of Light and Good, Master of the Law, Father of Khors and Lord of the Horizons, Slayer of Ptah, Osiris, and Isis, and Patron of the Dwarves (<em>Southlands</em> 233)
  Heretical Aten - Father of Fire (<em>Southlands</em> 233)
  Bastet – Goddess of Cats and Hunters, Queen of Perfumes, Bastard Child of Aten, Mother of Alchemy, Patron of the Gnolls, and Wife of Anu-Akma (<em>Southlands</em> 235)
  Djyy (Veles) – World Serpent, God of the Earth and Waters, Creator of the World, Father of Serpents, Lord of Oceans, Emperor of Earthquakes, Patron of Giants, Lizardfolk, and Dragons, Voice of Distant Stars, and Patron of Lignas (<em>Southlands</em> 236)
  Eshu – God of Travelers and Nomads, Patron of Weavers, Master of Birds, Luckbringer, the Golden Gifter, Guide over the Plains, Father of the Ushabti, and Friend to the Jinnborn and the Luckless (<em>Southlands</em> 237)
  Horus – Sky Lord, Master of the Sun, the Moon, and the Heavens, the Desert Falcon, Prince of Princes, the Majestic One, the Chieftain, the Vigilant, the Phoenix God, the True King, and Patron of Nuria Natal (<em>Southlands</em> 238)
  Isis – The Golden Goddess of Dawn, Love, and Mercy, the Gentle Maiden, Lady of the Healing Hand, Daughter of Aten, Mother of Horus, Mistress of the Petal Palm, and Protector of Children (<em>Southlands</em> 240)
  Kwansi – The Spider God, Dancer on the Shores of Time, the Mystic Spider, Storyteller of the Gods, Patron of Seers and Oracles, Friend to the Footloose, God of Laughter, and the Night Hunter (<em>Southlands</em> 241)
  Mbanu – Forge of the Dwarves, Lord of Law, the Hammer God, Iron Fists, God of the Fireproof Beard, and Master of Flames and Lord of Light (<em>Southlands</em> 242)
  Ninkash – Mother of Beer, Goddess of Merriment, Patron of Brewers and Tavern Keepers, and Matron Goddess of the Cantonal Dwarves (<em>Southlands</em> 243)
  Ogun – The Warrior God, Mighty Lord of Iron and War, Patron of the Morreg, Hunter of the Divine Spheres, Forest Master, Patron of Smiths and Miners, Keeper of Keys and Dungeons, Judge of Truth and Celestial Jailer, and Friend to Eshu (<em>Southlands</em> 244)
  Ptah – First and Reborn Creator-God of Dwarves and Men, Lord of the Eternal, Master of Justice, Sculptor of the Earth, Patron of the Dwarves, Husband to Ninkash and Sekhmet, Shipbuilder of the Gods, Tomb Builder of the God-Kings, and Lord of the Labyrinth (<em>Southlands</em> 245)
  Sabateus – Lord of Stars and Planets, Maker of Magic, Patron of the Shadow Paths, King of the Moon and Master of Night, and Lord of the Desert Night (<em>Southlands</em> 247)
  Takhar – Guardian of the Gates, Keeper of the Springs of Life and Death, Warden of the World Tree, Far-Seer, and the Incorruptible (<em>Southlands</em> 248)
  Thoth-Hermes – The Wise, God of Knowledge and Learning, Creator of Language, Lord of Merchants, Patron of Scholars and Thieves, Master of the Arcane Realms, and Creator of the Emerald Tablets (<em>Southlands</em> 249)
  Xevioso – God of War and Thunder, Lord of Battle and Rebirth, Patron of Narumbeki, Master of Strife, Swift Striding Commander, and Husband to the White Goddess (<em>Southlands</em> 250)
  Yemaja of the Waters – The Benevolent Voice, Goddess over All Waters, Mother of the Titans, Patroness of the Tamasheq, Lady of Sirens, the Eternal Memory, and Sister-Wife of Veles (<em>Southlands</em> 252)
  Aposis – The Chaos Serpent, Dragon of the Apocalypse, the Devouring Wyrm, Patron of Zanskar (<em>Southlands</em> 254)
  Arbeyach – Prince of Swarms, Arch-Devil of the Buzzing Hell Bzeletalet, Lord of Locusts, Patron of the Tosculi, Emperor of Wasps, Supreme General of the Meat-Raids, Scion of Endless Hunger, and Shining Light of Hives (<em>Southlands</em> 255)
  Baal-Hotep – He Who Rides on the Clouds, Lord of the Heavens, Lord of Fire and Master of Noble Sacrifice, King of All Dragons, Lord of Fertile Fields, Master of Rain and Dew, Scarlet Protector of the Innocent, Fearsome Judge of the Unrighteous, Supreme Fire Dragon, and Patron of the Empire and Dragonkin (<em>Southlands</em> 256)
  The Hunter – Master of the Hunt, the Horned Huntsman, the Blood God, the Horseman, the Many-skinned Walker, and Patron of Per-Kush (<em>Southlands</em> 257)
  Laughing Nkishi – The Laughing Darkness, Blood-muzzle, Man-killer, the One Who Knows the Path, the Two-faced God, Patron of the Gnolls (<em>Southlands</em> 258)
  Mot – God of Eternal Death, Lord of the Undead, the Death of Fire, Black Emperor of the Silent Land of Mirey, Prince of Necromancers, and High Potentate of Dragonslayers (<em>Southlands</em> 260)
  Nakresh – The Many-handed, Patron of Thieves and Tomb Robbers, Archmagus among Wizards, Demon Monkey and Bane of the Rakshasa, King of Revelry and Japes, Protector of the Poor and Destitute, and Bane of the Rich Man (<em>Southlands</em> 261)
  Selket – Goddess of Scorpions, Queen of Vipers, Mistress of the Desert, Shield of the Pure, Terror of the Faithless, Patron Goddess of Raiders and Nomads, and Mother of Venom (<em>Southlands</em> 262)
  Set – God of Storms and Chaos, True Patron of Nuria Natal, Son of Veles, Master of Men and Serpents, Lord of the Red Desert Lands, Wind Caller, Doom of Osiris, Friend to Strangers, Strongest of the Divine Company, and Defender of the Boat of the Sun (<em>Southlands</em> 263)
  White Goddess – Goddess of Bright Pain, the Sun’s Queen, the Pale Matriarch of Blood and Strength, Patron Goddess of the Orcs, and Empress of the Green Abyss (<em>Southlands</em> 264)
  
greyhawk_factions
  Pelor (Face in a sun, Neutral Good – God of sun, light, and strength. The Shining One, the Sun Father.)
  Ehlonna (Unicorn's Horn, Neutral Good – God of forests, woodlands, flora, fauna, and fertility. Ehlenestra.)
  Boccob (Eye in a pentagram, Neutral – God of magic, arcane knowledge, balance, and foresight. Lord of all magics, archmage of deities.)
  Kord (Eight pointed star of weapons, Chaotic Good – God of athletics, sports, brawling, strength, and courage.)
  Nerull (Skull and scythe, Neutral Evil – God of death, darkness, murder, and the underworld. The Reaper, Foe of All Good, Hater of Life, Bringer of Darkness.)
  Erythnul (Red blood drop, Chaotic Evil – God of hate, envy, malice, panic, ugliness, and slaughter. The Many.)
  Olidammara (Grinning mask, Chaotic Neutral – God of music, revels, wine, rogues, humor, and tricks. The Laughing Rogue.)
  Fharlanghn (Disk with horizon line, Neutral – God of horizons, distance, travel, and roads.)
  Wee Jas (Skull in Fireball, Lawful Neutral – God of magic, death, vanity, and law.)
  Obad-Hai (Mask of leaves, Neutral – God of nature, woodlands, freedom, hunting, beasts.)
  Hextor (Black spiked gauntlet with holding arrows, Lawful Evil – God of war, discord, massacres, conflict, fitness, and tyranny.)
  Heironeous (Lightning bolt, Lawful Good – God of chivalry, justice, honor, war, daring, and valor.)
  Istus (Webspinner, Neutral – Goddess of fate, destiny, divination, future, and honesty.)
  Kurell (Clutching hand, Chaotic Neutral – God of jealousy, revenge, thievery, and betrayal.)
  Ralishaz (Three bone-casting sticks, Chaotic Neutral – God of ill luck, misfortune, randomness, and madness.)
  Saint Cuthbert (Starburst, Lawful Neutral – God of common sense, wisdom, zeal, honesty, truth, and discipline.)
  Iuz (Skull with burning eyes, Neutral Evil – God of pain, oppression, evil, tyranny, and deceit.)
  Delleb (Open book, Lawful Good – God of reason, intellect, and study.)
  Trithereon (Triskelion of avenging angels, Chaotic Good – God of individuality, liberty, retribution, and self-defense.)
  Pholtus (Silver sun on a blue field, Lawful Good – God of light, resolution, law, order, inflexibility, and sun/moon.)
  Procan (Wave and trident, Chaotic Neutral – God of seas, sea life, salt, sea weather, and navigation.)
  Zilchus (Hand clutching a bag of gold, Lawful Neutral – God of power, prestige, money, business, and influence.)
  Beory (Green disk, Neutral – Goddess of the Oerth, nature, and rain.)
  Ulaa (Hammer and mountain, Lawful Good – Goddess of hills, mountains, and gemstones.)
  Wenta (Golden cup and grape vine, Chaotic Good – Goddess of autumn, west wind, harvest, and brewing.)
  Knights of the Hart (Stag head – Order dedicated to justice, righteousness, and protection of the common folk.)
  Scarlet Brotherhood (Red handprint – Secret society seeking to expand their influence and power.)
  The Iron League (Interlocked iron rings – Alliance formed to oppose the Great Kingdom's imperialistic ambitions.)
  The Seekers (Open eye – Group dedicated to seeking and preserving ancient knowledge and artifacts.)
  The Silent Ones (Hooded figure – Mysterious organization known for their secrecy and magical prowess.)
  Rangers of the Gnarley Forest (Green tree on a brown field – Rangers tasked with protecting the Gnarley Forest and its inhabitants.)
  The Horned Society (Horned skull – Powerful and evil organization known for their diabolical schemes.)
  The Circle of Eight (Eight-pointed star – Group of powerful wizards dedicated to balance and opposing evil.)
  The Green Dragon Brotherhood (Green dragon head – Organization known for its cunning, ambition, and ties to draconic lore.)
  Lordship of the Isles (Three crossed swords – Collection of islands and their ruling noble class.)
  The Church of Zilchus (Golden coin with Zilchus' face – Religious organization dedicated to the teachings and worship of Zilchus.)
  The Wild Coast Confederation (Wild boar head – Confederation of free towns and cities along the Wild Coast.)
  Doomgrinder Cult (Broken gear, Lawful Evil – Cult worshiping an ancient and malevolent entity known as the Doomgrinder.)
  The Ulek States (Three stars over a mountain range – Group of states known for their democratic governance and resistance to tyranny.)
  The Thieves' Guild of Greyhawk (Black mask – Organization of thieves operating within the city of Greyhawk.)
  The Plar of Littleberg (Shepherd's crook – Ruler of the small, peaceful town of Littleberg.)
  Ahlsheyan Mercenaries (Two crossed swords over a shield – Group of skilled mercenaries known for their discipline and effectiveness.)
  The Rhennee Bargesfolk (Barge on a river – Nomadic people known for their river-based lifestyle and trading.)
  Society of Magi (Interlocked circles – Group of mages dedicated to magical research and the sharing of arcane knowledge.)
